basic/basic-01.agda-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
basic/basic-01.agda-
basic/basic-01.agda-proof₀ : Γ ⊢ subgoal₀
basic/basic-01.agda-proof₀ =
basic/basic-01.agda-  (RAA
basic/basic-01.agda:    (atp-canonicalize ⊥
basic/basic-01.agda-      (assume {Γ = Γ}
basic/basic-01.agda-        (¬ subgoal₀))))

basic/basic-04.agda-  (RAA
basic/basic-04.agda-    (atp-simplify ⊥
basic/basic-04.agda-      (assume {Γ = Γ}
basic/basic-04.agda-        (¬ subgoal₀))
basic/basic-04.agda:      (atp-canonicalize p
basic/basic-04.agda-        (weaken (¬ subgoal₀)
basic/basic-04.agda-          (assume {Γ = ∅} a₁)))))
basic/basic-04.agda-
basic/basic-04.agda-proof : Γ ⊢ goal
basic/basic-04.agda-proof =
--
--
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-proof₀ =
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-  (RAA
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-    (atp-resolve ⊥ p
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-      (atp-resolve p q
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-        (atp-conjunct q
biconditional/bicond-01.agda:          (atp-canonicalize ((¬ p) ∧ q)
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-            (assume {Γ = Γ}
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-              (¬ subgoal₀))))
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-        (atp-conjunct ((¬ q) ∨ p)
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-          (atp-clausify (((¬ p) ∨ q) ∧ ((¬ q) ∨ p))
--
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-            (assume {Γ = Γ}
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-              (¬ subgoal₀))))
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-        (atp-conjunct ((¬ q) ∨ p)
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-          (atp-clausify (((¬ p) ∨ q) ∧ ((¬ q) ∨ p))
biconditional/bicond-01.agda:            (atp-canonicalize ((¬ p) ⇔ (¬ q))
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-              (weaken (¬ subgoal₀)
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-                (assume {Γ = ∅} a₁))))))
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-      (atp-conjunct (¬ p)
--
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-              (weaken (¬ subgoal₀)
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-                (assume {Γ = ∅} a₁))))))
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-      (atp-conjunct (¬ p)
biconditional/bicond-01.agda:        (atp-canonicalize ((¬ p) ∧ q)
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-          (assume {Γ = Γ}
biconditional/bicond-01.agda-            (¬ subgoal₀))))))

biconditional/bicond-02.agda-proof₀ =
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-  (RAA
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-    (atp-resolve ⊥ r
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-      (atp-resolve r q
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-        (atp-conjunct q
biconditional/bicond-02.agda:          (atp-canonicalize ((¬ r) ∧ q)
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-            (assume {Γ = Γ}
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-              (¬ subgoal₀))))
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-        (atp-conjunct ((¬ q) ∨ r)
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-          (atp-clausify (((¬ q) ∨ r) ∧ ((¬ r) ∨ q))
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-            (atp-simplify ((¬ q) ⇔ (¬ r))
--
--
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-            (assume {Γ = Γ}
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-              (¬ subgoal₀))))
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-        (atp-conjunct ((¬ q) ∨ r)
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-          (atp-clausify (((¬ q) ∨ r) ∧ ((¬ r) ∨ q))
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-            (atp-simplify ((¬ q) ⇔ (¬ r))
biconditional/bicond-02.agda:              (atp-canonicalize ((¬ p) ⇔ ((¬ q) ⇔ r))
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-                (weaken (¬ subgoal₀)
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-                  (assume {Γ = [ a₁ ]} a₂)))
--
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-                (weaken (¬ subgoal₀)
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-                  (assume {Γ = [ a₁ ]} a₂)))
biconditional/bicond-02.agda:              (atp-canonicalize p
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-                (weaken-Δ₁
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-                  (∅ , a₂ , ¬ subgoal₀)
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-                  (assume {Γ = ∅} a₁)))))))
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-      (atp-conjunct (¬ r)
--
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-                (weaken-Δ₁
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-                  (∅ , a₂ , ¬ subgoal₀)
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-                  (assume {Γ = ∅} a₁)))))))
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-      (atp-conjunct (¬ r)
biconditional/bicond-02.agda:        (atp-canonicalize ((¬ r) ∧ q)
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-          (assume {Γ = Γ}
biconditional/bicond-02.agda-            (¬ subgoal₀))))))
